 While addressing the country on the evening of 31 December 2016, the Prime Minister did not announce a loan waiver for the farmers but announced an interest waiver for them
 maafee kii yah yojana sabhi kisaanon ke liye nahin thi
 Sixty days interest will be paid by the farmers who have taken loans from district cooperative banks and primary societies
 kisaanon ke karz ke liye 21,000 karod kii atirikt raashi uplabdh karai jaaegi
 20,000 crores will be made available through NABARD
 yani saath din kaa sirf byaaz maaf hua
 The loan was not waived, rather the loan amount was further increased so that farmers could take more loans
 is baar ke bajet main das lakh karod ke krishi rin kaa praavdhaan kiya he
 The record in itself
 kisaanon ko karz kii to kami nahin hogi magar yahaan sawaal karz maafee kaa he
 State Bank of India has recently announced a one-time settlement scheme for farm equipment and tractor loans
 isamen bank tractor lone vene vaale kisaanon ko 40 fisadi chhot de saktaa he
 Those borrowers up to 25 lakh will get the benefit of this scheme
 bank ko lagata he ki 6000 karod lone kaa lautnaa mushkil he, isliye kuch riyaayat dekar paise kii vasuuli kii jaae jisase unki recovery bad sake
 The farmers of Uttar Pradesh have given full support to the BJP
 indian express ke harish damodaran ne apane adhyayan se bataaya he ki pehle do charan ke 168 vidhansabha kshetron kii pahchaan ganna kisaanon or aalu ke kisaanon ke rup main he
 BJP has won 83 of the 106 seats in the sugarcane belt
 tab jabaki march das tak chini milon ne ganna kisaanon ke kareeb chaar hazaar karod nahin chukaaye the
 Farmers in this belt also reported their problems due to demonetisation
 aalu belt kii 62 siton main se 50 par bijepi jiti he
 Potato was being sold 700-800 per quintal before demonetisation
 notebandi ke baad aalu kaa bhav gikar 300-400 prati quintal par aa gaya
 But when the electoral result came, bjp's bumper crop started waving
 notebandi ke baad bhi kisaanon ne pradhanmantri modi par bharosa kiya he
 BJP will not break the trust of this new electorate
 16 march ke financial times main karmvari singh ne likhaa he ki chote or seemaant kisaanon ko saarvajanik kshetron ke bainkon ne 85,000 karod kaa lone diya he
 The state treasury may not have that much money
 kya centre sarkaar upi ke kisaanon kaa 85,000 karod maaf karegi?tippaniyan On Thursday itself, Agriculture Minister Radha Mohan Singh has said in the Lok Sabha that the central government will bear the burden of loan waiver of UP farmers
 sarkaar patibaddh he
 It is quite different that farmers do not benefit from loan waiver
 2009 ke baad karj maafee ho rahi he to aisa bhi nahin he ki ek baar maaf kar dene par har saal kisaan isaki maang karte hi hai or sarkaar bhi maan leti he
 The plan of amnesty after eight-nine years shows that both the government and the farmers want to repay the loan, but given the depth of their crisis, the plan to forgive intermittently is not that bad
 bainkon par enpie yani non proffit asset kaa pehle se dabaav badhata ja rahaa he
 The NPA has doubled in the last 15 months as the industry is unable to repay the loan
 sitambar 2015 main 3,49,556 karod tha jo sitambar 2016 main 6,68,825 karod ho gaya
 On March 15, the Finance Minister said that the NPA growth in the March quarter has come to a halt as the steel sector is starting to improve
 bhartiya rigerv bank ke aankadon ke anusaar bank ko enpie kii vasuuli main kaaphi dikkat aa rahi he
 18 of the total NPA in March 2014
 4 fisadi vasula ja sakaa tha
 Total NPA recovery reduced to 10 in March 2016
 3 fisadi ho gai
 That is, the recovery is reduced
 bainkon ke enpie ke kaaran bhi yah tark chal padataa he ki jab udyogpatiyon ke lakhon karod nahin vasule ja rahe hai to kisaanon ke bhi lone maaf hone chahie
 Like an economist, this is a problem
 kisi bhi sarkaar ke liye itane lakh karod maaf kar dene main vyaavhaarik or saidhantik dikkat bhi he
 But you cannot see political decisions this way
 kheti kaa lone maaf karne se karz kaa anushaasan tuutata he
 No one else but Arundhati Bhattacharya, head of the country's largest bank, has said that farmers should be supported, but not at the cost of loan discipline
 hamen isse baahar nikalnaa chahie
 Former Reserve Bank Governor Raghuram Rajan had also said that it is not right to waive farmers' debts
 isse kisaan ko nuksaan hi hota he
 As soon as the SBI chief heard the statement, the Congress mlas reached the headquarters of State Bank of India and demonstrated

 rajya sarkaar kyon nahin karz maaf kar rahi he
 The Shiv Sena is also supporting this demand of the opposition
 31 disambar 2016 kii shaam pradhanmantri ne desh ko sambodhit karte hue kisaanon ke liye karj maafee kaa elaan to nahin kiya magar unke liye byaaz maafee kii ghoshnaa zarur kii
 This scheme of amnesty was not for all farmers
 jin kisaanon ne zila sahakaarita bainkon or primary sosayadi se lone liya he, unke saath dinon kaa byaaz sarkaar bharegi
 An additional amount of 21,000 crore will be made available for the loan of farmers
 naabard ke zariye 20,000 karod or uplabdh karaaye jaaenge
 That means only the interest of sixty days is forgiven
 karza maaf nahin hua balki karz dene kii raashi or badha di gai taaki kisaan or lone le saken
 a provision of ten million crore agricultural loans has been made in this budget
 apane aap main record he
 There will be no shortage of loans to farmers, but the question here is about loan waiver
 state bank of india ne haal hi main kheti ke upkaran or tractor lone ke liye ek baar main setelment skim kaa elaan kiya he
 In this, the bank can give 40% rebate to farmers who own tractor loans
 25 lakh tak ke lone lene waalon ko is skim kaa laabh milegaa
 The bank feels that it is difficult to return 6000 crores loan, so the money can be recovered by giving some concession so that their recovery can be increased
 uttar pradesh ke kisaanon ne bijepi kaa bharpoor saath diya he
 Harish Damodaran of the Indian Express has told from his study that 168 assembly constituencies of the first two phases have been identified as sugarcane farmers and potato farmers
 ganna belt kii 106 siton main se 83 siten bijepi ne jeet lee hai
 Then, till March 10, the sugar mills had not paid nearly four thousand crores to the sugarcane farmers
 is belt main bhi kisaanon ne notebandi ke chalate apni pareshaani bataai thi
 The BJP won 50 of the 62 seats in the potato belt
 notebandi se pehle aalu 700-800 prati quintal bik rahaa tha
 After demonetisation, the price of potato came down to 300-400 per quintal
 par chunavi nateeja aayaa to bijepi kii banpar fasal lahalhane lagi
 Even after demonetisation, farmers have relied on Prime Minister Modi
 bijepi apane is nae matadaata varg kaa bharosa to nahin todegi
 In the Financial Times of March 16, Karmavari Singh wrote that public sector banks have given loans of 85,000 crore to small and marginal farmers
 rajya ke khajaane main shaayad itnaa paisa na ho
 Will the central government forgive 85,000 crore of UP farmers? guuruuvaar ko hi krishi mantri radha mohan singh ne loksabhaa main to kaha hi he ki centre sarkaar upi ke kisaanon kii karj maafee kaa bhaar uthaaegi
 The government is committed
 yah baat bilkul alag he ki kisaanon ko karj maafee se laabh nahin hota
 After 2009, if the debt is being forgiven, then it is not that once it is forgiven, the farmers demand it every year and the government also agrees
 aath nau saal ke baad maafee kii yojana se pataa chalata he ki sarkaar or kisaan donon lone chukaana bhi chaahate hai magar unke sankat kii gaharaai ko dekhte hue bich bich main maaf kar dene kii yojana utani bhi karaab nahin he
 The pressure on npas or non-profit assets is already increasing on banks
 udyog jagat karz nahin chukaa paa rahaa he lihaaza pichley 15 maheene main enpie dugana ho gaya he
 3,49,556 crore in September 2015 which increased to 6,68,825 crore in September 2016
 15 march ko vitt mantri ne kaha he ki march kii timahi main enpie kaa badhanaa kuch thama he kyonki steel sector main sudhaar hone laga he
 According to the Reserve Bank of India data, the bank is facing difficulty in recovery of npas
 march 2014 main kul enpie kaa 18
 4 percent was recovered
 march 2016 main kul enpie kii vasuuli ghatakar 10
 3 percent
 yani recovery kam ho gai

 arthshaastri kii tarah dekhenge to yah ek samasya he

 haal main jahaan tak yaaddasht jaati he aisa koi vidhansabha chunaav nahin rahaa hoga jisamen itani badi sankhya main patrakaron ne har chunavi utaar-chadhaav ko siyaasi microscope se is tarah ankhen gada kar dekha ho
 i spent the last 15 days traveling to different parts of western Uttar Pradesh, Bundelkhand and Awadh
 in yatraaon ke dauraan mujhe amit shah, rajnath singh, akhilesh yadav, mulaayam singh yadav, prashanth kishor or upi chunaav ke kuch or ahm diggajon ke saath vakt bitaane kaa mauka mila

 Based on what i have experienced, i am concluding what has happened so far and what may change in the last four steps
 hameshaa ki tarah is baar bhi meraa chopping block par apni gardan rakhane kaa iraadaa nahin he, isliye main ye anumaan lagane se bachuungaa ki meri raay main koun jeet rahaa he
 In the following squeeze, i will limit myself to the extent of any non-partisan observer
 1
 bjp's future in UP Ticker on Hindu solidarity, the Prime Minister may have ignited the 'graveyard vs
 cremation ghat' debate in Fatehpur on Sunday, but communal resonance was heard loudly in the speeches of all other BJP leaders
 is
 bijepi kaa mukhya jor isi baat par rahaa he ki samaajawaadee party sarkaar ne beete 5 saal alpsankhyak samudaay ke tushtikaran main hi bitaye or ab chizon ko durust karne kaa vakt he
 The important lesson that the BJP has learned from the humiliating defeat in Bihar is that the party continued to present development as an important issue, while the strong caste arithmetic of Lalu and Nitish completely submerged the saffron party's prospects
 amit shah ne 2014 jaise gaiyr yadav anya pichhadaa varg (OBC) or ati pichhadaa varg (MBC) ko ekajute kar bihar main jo bachi-khuchi ummid laga rakhi thi us par mohan bhagwat ke aarakshan sambandhi bayaan ne pani pher diya tha
 While spending the whole day with Amit Shah in different parts of Bundelkhand, he saw that Shah got the most applause and support during the campaign only when he spoke of banning abattoirs in the state
 shah kaa aarope he ki akhilesh sarkaar ke dauraan boojadkhaanon ko bade paimaane par panpane kaa mauka mila
 Earlier it was limited to western Uttar Pradesh, but now it has spread to other parts of UP as well
 shah kaa aarope he ki in boojadkhaanon main anya pashuon ke saath chori-chupe gaayon kaa bhi vadh hota he
 Along with the promise to ban slaughterhouses, BJP is also vigorously raising the issue of triple talaq
 party saath hi aarope laga rahi he ki laptop vitaran main akhilesh apane samarthakon ko lekar pakshpaati rahe
 The BJP leadership did not hesitate at all about the communal put in the party's campaign
 hinduon se apni dharmik pahchaan ko mastishk main sabase upar rakh kar vot karaayaa ja sake, yahi bijepi ke liye upi jeetne kii kunjee he
 Based on the feedback the BJP has received from the first three phases of voting, the party believes that it has done enough work to unite the Hindu forces on a larger scale and this will be able to beat the minority-backed opposition
 2
 Reaction to the aggressive appearances of minorities regarding support, according to reports from parts of West Uttar Pradesh, Muslim youths took out rallies on motorcycles in cities and towns in support of the sp-congress alliance
 is ghatnakram se gathbandhan ke un manageron ko bechaini hui jo chaahate the ki alpsankhyak samudaay samaajawaadee party or congress ko samarthan dene ko lekar bahut zyada mukhar nahin dikhe
 Coalition strategists want Muslims to remain calm and not express their support openly
 isaki jagah wo matdaan vaale din gathbandhan ke liye jaakar vot den
 Initially, there were some doubts about who the minorities would vote for
 lekin pehle teen charnon ke matdaan ke jo trend saamne aae unke mutabik alpsankhyakon ne adhiktar gathbandhan kaa hi samarthan kiya
 As an exception, those seats can be named where the BSP fielded strong minority candidates
 gathbandhan ke ek top ranneetikaar kehete hai ki 'dharmanirpeksh gathbandhan' ke liye alpsankhyak samarthan vaisaa majboot to nahin dikhaa jaisaa ki bihar main dikhaa tha, lekin muslimon kaa voting kaa rujhaan adhiktar gathbandhan ke paksh main hi dikhaa
 The BJP showed full force in spreading that minorities are voting for a large number of alliances and Hindus should unite to prevent the alliance from winning
 alpsankhyakon kii ore se samarthan kaa aakraamak pradarshan bahusankhyak samudaay kii maansikta par asar daalata he or isse kuch voter prabhavit ho sakate hai
 The level of polarization is not the same as that seen after the Muzaffarnagar riots, but Hindu solidarity is certainly a big factor in this assembly election
 agar bijepi phinishing line ko pehle paar karne main kaamyaab rahati he to uski jeet ke peeche bahusankhyak ekajutata kaa ahm haath rahegaa
 3
 bhaiyameniayak aisa rajya, jahaan shashan tedi kheer mana jaataa he, vahaan kisi mukhyamantri kaa kaarykaal puraa hote hote tej satta virdohi lahar chalanaa swaabhaavik mana jaataa he
 This has been happening with Chief Ministers of all parties for two decades now
 hakeekat to ye he ki bahut se raajnneetik pandit bhi is baar sanshay main hai ki aakhir upi main hoga kya
 Such a situation can mainly be attributed to the positive image of Akhilesh Yadav, whom his supporters call Bhaiya
 aise matadaata bhi jo akhilesh ko vot dene kaa iraadaa nahin karte wo bhi akhilesh ke bare main zyada kuch nakaaratmak kehane kii sthiti main nahin hai
 Akhilesh's rallies across UP can be seen by the mob of his zealous young supporters
 yuvaaon, khaas taur par yadavon or muslimon main bhaiyamenia andar tak paith kar gaya he
 Akhilesh's image among supporters is like a political rockstar
 akhilesh pehle yadav netaa hai jinhone apni party ke paaramparik vot bank se itar logon main apane liye sakaaratmak chhavi banaai he
 Whether Akhilesh wins or loses, it is certain that he will remain an axis in the politics of Uttar Pradesh for a long time
 piem modi kii tarah akhilesh ne bhi marketing main master class lee lagati he
 Throughout the campaign, Akhilesh kept his message positive
 us nakaaratmakataa se khud ko dur rakhaa jiskaa sahaara unke virdohi un par hamale karne ke liye lete rahe hai
 Akhilesh has changed the face of Lucknow
 agra-lakhanu express ve ke atirikt sadakon kii sthiti pehle se behatar hui he lekin ab bhi upi kii sadaken desh main sabase badtar hai
 Generating employment is a big problem in UP, while the rapidly growing population is getting desperate in search of employment
 4
 The brightest glow of Modi's star Narendra Modi's tenure as Prime Minister is going to be completed for about 3 years, but Modi's charm has not decreased
 is samvaadadaata ne 2014 ke prachaar abhiyaan ke dauraan bhi modi kii kai reliyaan sunin
 When compared to the hysterical peak of the 2014 campaign, there has been a slight decrease in the level of enthusiasm but still the eagerness for Modi remains
 ek pradhanmantri ke liye jo apane aadhe kaarykaal ke bich main he ye uplabdhi ullekhneey he
 The middle of the term is the time when the anti-incumbency trend begins to happen, but this virus has not yet bitten Modi
 achche din beshak naa aae hon lekin logon ko ab bhi pradhanmantri par bahut bharosa he
 He believes that the solution of India's problems lies with the Prime Minister
 upi kii jang aakhir koi bhi jite lekin 2019 ke aam chunaav main modi ko haraana vipaksh ke liye asambhav se kam nahin hoga
 5
 bijepi notebandi ko zyada tool dene ke paksh main nahinsaakshatkaaron main bijepi netaa beshak kehete rahen ki agar 2017 chunaav ko notebandi par janadesh mana jaataa he to unhen koi dikkat nahin
 On the other hand, the ground reality is that the BJP leadership is trying its best not to remind people of the pain of demonetisation
 maine amit shah ke saath jo puraa din bitaayaa, usamen unhone chaar reliyon ko sambodhit kiya or ek baar bhi kahin notebandi kaa zikr nahin kiya
 Home Minister Rajnath Singh spoke on the ban on bonding but that too at the end of the meeting, in the style of Khanapurti
 bijepi matadaataaon ko notebandi ke phaaydon par aashwast karne kii jagah unhen aage badhane kaa sandesh dena chaahati he
 The BJP wants voters to understand that the pain they have suffered is in the national interest and in the coming years it will benefit the economy
 6
 No impact of demonetisation on elections
 Opponents of Modi, especially Rahul Gandhi, spent big time reminding people about the pain of demonetisation
 ve chaahate the ki is chunaav main notebandi mukhya mudda bane
 But this did not happen
 vyapaaree samudaay notebandi ko un par thopane ke liye beshak bijepi se naakhush he, lekin unke modi ke virodhiyon ko vot dene kii sambhaavna nahin ke baraabar he
 There have been reports that those who express their grief with loudness can stay away from the elections and decide not to vote due to unhappiness with BJP, but on the polling day this community appeared to vote for BJP
 bijepi kii gananaa ke hisaab se vyapaaree notebandi se zyada samaajwaadiyon ke tahat kanoon-vyavastha kii haalat ko naapsand karte hai
 Because of demonetisation, the number of people who vote against BJP is not enough to reverse the result of the election
 7
 While reforming the strategy, Rahul said while covering the Punjab election campaign, i am now again saying that Rahul Gandhi has already improved the art of speaking among the people
 ateet kii tulana main unke sandesh ab adhik dhardaar hai
 People are really listening to what Rahul Gandhi is saying in his rallies in this election
 sunne main ye atapata lage lekin is samvaadadaata ne 2014 prachaar abhiyaan ke dauraan khud dekha tha ki rahul gandhi jansabhaon main jaise hi bolnaa shuru karte the log uthakar chalanaa shuru kar dete the
 But now that situation is no more
 haalanki modi ko aap sunen to unki tulana main rahul fike lagane lagate hai
 We heard both at Hardoi district in UP at a gap of two hours
 sidhaa kahen to donon main koi tulana nahin he
 Rahul's father Rajiv Gandhi was also not an orator of Hindi but he did not have an image like Modi as an opponent
 praytn karne ke baavjood rahul gandhi ke paas modi kii ghor vakpatutaa kii kaat nahin he
 8
 rajnath ne kabhi bijepi kaa siem cheharaa banane se inkaar nahin kiyabijepi main andarkhaane aisi baat uchhal kar saamne aane kii charchaa thi ki rajnath singh ko upi main siem ke liye party kaa cheharaa ban kar jane ke liye kaha ja saktaa he, lekin grih mantri ne dilli chhodane ke liye manaa kar diya
 But this proved to be mere speculation
 is samvaadadaata ke paas aisa maanane ke kaaran maujuud hai ki rajnath singh ko na to modi or na hi shah ne upi main party kaa cheharaa ban kar jane ke liye kaha
 According to sources close to the Home Minister, if he had been formally made such a proposal, he would have positively accepted it
 bijepi kaa tark ye najar aata he ki thakur jaise savarna, jis samudaay se rajnath aate hai, kisi bhi surat main party kaa hi samarthan karenge
 One of the main efforts of the modi-shah team is to increase the scope of bjp's appeal to non-yadav obcs and Backward Classes (MBC)
 party kaa ganit ye he ki keshav prasad maury jaise vyakti ko aage kar kushvaha jaise pichde virgon main samarthan badhaayaa ja saktaa he
 The counter argument of the above argument is that many voters who support Modi at the center are asking who is the bjp's face for CM in UP? Taking forward a leader like Rajnath for this would have helped in getting the answer to this question
 agar bijepi jitati he to ranneetikaar daawa kar sakate hai ki unka game-plan kargar rahaa
 If the BJP stays away from victory, questions will arise whether it was a sense of insecurity that prevented the tallest leader in UP from becoming the face of the party's CM
 9
